Following pluriverse entity decided to intervene into collective: BitTorrent Tit-for-Tat Mechanism
Reasoning: The BitTorrent Tit-for-Tat Mechanism is central to addressing both the desires and fears of the group. It incentivizes peers to upload by offering faster download speeds in return, which directly aligns with the desire to have active and cooperative peers for faster downloads and to optimize download rates. Moreover, it mitigates fears related to free-riding behavior and unfair reciprocation, as it establishes a system of reciprocity that encourages cooperation among peers. By ensuring that peers are rewarded for their contributions, the Tit-for-Tat mechanism helps maintain stable session lengths and improves overall connectivity in the network.

If you decide to leave this resolution, it may be collapsed due to departure of all participants and you won't be able to get the benefits it provided. Интернет-провайдеры declined the resolution proposed by End-user with reasoning: While the proposal aims to improve internet speed and reliability through decentralized user-centric paradigms, it raises concerns regarding control over network infrastructure and potential loss of revenue. Allowing end-users to become autonomous nodes could lead to unpredictable traffic patterns and legal issues, undermining the stability and profitability that 'Интернет-провайдеры' currently strive to maintain. Additionally, the reliance on personal quantum computing devices may not be feasible for all users, potentially creating a divide in service quality.
